    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">How can small businesses launch and promote loyalty programs effectively? ü§î

Launching a <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Floyalty&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#loyalty</a> program doesn‚Äôt have to be complicated! Here are some key steps small businesses can take to ensure success:

üü¶ Make sure your loyalty program is easy to understand and join. Customers should be able to participate without hassle
üü¶ Let your customers know about the benefits of joining. Use emails, social media, and in-store promotions to spread the word.
üü¶ Tailor rewards based on your customers' preferences to make them feel valued and special. This will increase engagement and loyalty.
üü¶ Keep your customers excited about the program by regularly updating offers and communicating with them. 

Reach out to Appcent to launch your loyalty program today!

        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Did you know how global brands implement their loyalty programs? Here‚Äôs an inspiring example: <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fstarbucks&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Starbucks</a> üßã

When you think of Starbucks, delicious coffee may come to mind, but there's another key to their success ‚Äì their loyalty program! üèÖ

Starbucks introduced a <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Ftiered&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#tiered</a> rewards system through their Starbucks Rewards program, using "Stars" as their point currency. This system is designed to encourage different ways to participate and earn more rewards.

üí°This smart loyalty strategy did more than just offer rewards ‚Äî it created an engaging experience that encouraged customers to return more often and spend more. The result? A 7% increase in sales and stronger customer loyalty.

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Fintech Software Development in Numbers üî¢

<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/gartner?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Gartner</a>‚Äôs recent insights offer a deep dive into the trends and challenges shaping fintech software development!

Here are the key insights: 
üî∏ Security and integration remain key hurdles for finance software buyers.
üî∏ 72% of finance businesses are increasing their software budgets, with IT security and management as top priorities.
üî∏ 67% of finance companies require 3-6 months to select new software, with reviews playing a critical role.
üî∏ 70% of buyers report regret, driven by unexpected costs and excessive complexity.
üî∏ 31% attempted to renegotiate contracts due to regret, while 28% opted to cancel entirely.

These insights highlight the need for clear, scalable solutions in fintech software development. As finance organizations continue their digital transformation journeys, making informed software choices will be key to achieving sustainable growth. 

Appcent is here to help you navigate this path with tailored, secure, and efficient solutions! üì±
